<!-- EDITABLE: The page title -->
<h1 class="science">Mouse MitoCarta3.0: 1140 mitochondrial genes</h1>

<p>
The MitoCarta3.0 mouse inventory is a collection of 1140 nuclear and mtDNA genes encoding proteins with strong support of mitochondrial localization. This table provides a summary of evidence supporting mitochondrial localization, the protein distribution across 14 tissues, as well  as annotation of biological pathways (based on manual literature review) and sub-compartment (based on annotator's "best guess" integrating sequence features, experimental data, literature, and pathway context; note all subunits of protein complexes are assigned the same compartment).  The genes are ordered by strength of mitochondrial evidence. More complete information is available for download in file <a href="http://www.broadinstitute.org/ftp/distribution/metabolic/papers/Pagliarini/MitoCarta3.0/Mouse.MitoCarta3.0.xls">Mouse.MitoCarta3.0.xls</a>.  See also <a href="https://www.broadinstitute.org/node/652421/">MitoCarta3.0 home</a> for a description of the project and <a href="https://www.broadinstitute.org/node/652901/">MitoCarta3.0 documentation</a> for information on the columns below. 
</p>
<p></p>
